I've done this before, it does improve the strength and shine of your hair, so in that aspect yes it does work if used consistently. However, you should keep the jar loosely closed, like just set the lid on top, don't screw it on. Leave it for at least 3 days, at most 7 days (depending on your climate). It should smell slightly sour. Leaving rice in the water will make the fermentation process take longer. Do not heat the water after fermentation, it will kill all the good bacteria you just created. Also, dilute the rice water by half as it's pretty acidic if you let it ferment well, and you can either use as a spray on mask or rinse after shampoo and conditioner. Hope this helps!

How long will your hair grow and how long will it take
Nothing you put in your hair is going to make it grow faster/longer. Hair growth is mostly due to genetics. If any of these remedies works for you it is because you already have the genetics.  Masks and remedies can make your hair less likely to split and break which will help your hair grow long, but nothing will make your hair grow faster or longer than what your hair is programmed to do. This has been debunked many times.  Just eat healthy, drink water and treat your hair nicely and it will grow healthy. Simple as that.
